[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtika-core/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/utils/ProcessUtils.jav[0m[1;92ma:153[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m165[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m155[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m165[0m[39m:    public static FileProcessResult [0m[1;35mexecute[0m[1;39m([0m[39mProcessBuilder pb,[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtika-app/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/cli/TikaCLI.jav[0m[1;92ma:1090[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1095[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1090[0m[39m:        public void [0m[1;35mparseEmbedded[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTikaInputStream tis, ContentHandler [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontentHandler, Metadata metadata, boolean outputHtml[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws SAXException, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIOException [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1091[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1092[0m[39m:            MediaType contentType = [0m[1;35mdetector.detect[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtis, metadata[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1093[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1094[0m[39m:            String name = [0m[1;35mmetadata.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTikaCoreProperties.RESOURCE_NAME_KEY[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1095[0m[39m:            File outputFile = null;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause & Critical Logic[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The vulnerability stems from ShellCodeDetector’s use of ProcessBuilder to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectly execute a user‐supplied script file [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`tmpFile`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in its working directory. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSince the file contents are attacker‐controlled, this allows arbitrary code [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecution.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must preserve the “shebang” detection and the ability to distinguish [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“no‐arg” scripts [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexit code [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m from those requiring arguments, as downstream Tika [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic may adapt behavior based on the `SHELL_NO_ARGS` metadata.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We will not touch ProcessUtils or any harness/fuzzing code.  All changes live [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minside ShellCodeDetector.detect, affecting only how we invoke the external “shell” [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor syntax‐only checking.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Strategy Overview[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace the direct execution of `tmpFile` [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`new [0m[1;35mProcessBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfileName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith a controlled invocation of the system shell in “syntax‐check” mode.  Most [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mUnix‐style shells support a “‐n” [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno execute[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m flag: the shell will parse the script[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor syntax errors and return an exit code, but will not run any commands.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Construct the ProcessBuilder command array in a fixed, safe manner: [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m[[0m[39mshellExecutable, syntaxCheckFlag, “--”, sanitizedFileName[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.  The only untrusted [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata is the sanitized filename, and we guard against flag injection by inserting [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“--” before it.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - On non‐Unix platforms [0m[1;39m([0m[39mWindows[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, skip the dynamic check entirely: after [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshebang detection, conservatively set `SHELL_NO_ARGS` to false [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor true if we [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchoose[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but do not invoke external commands.  This avoids cross‐platform [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshell‐injection pitfalls and preserves build/tests.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Retain the existing call to `[0m[1;35mProcessUtils.execute[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpb, timeout, …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, so we [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleverage the same timeouts, buffer limits, and exit‐value capture logic.  Only the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munderlying `ProcessBuilder` invocation changes.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Steps[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In ShellCodeDetector.detect [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m88[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m106[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. After writing the temp file [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`tmpFile`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and before creating the [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mProcessBuilder:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         • Determine if the platform is Unix‐like or Windows [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., via [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mSystem.getProperty[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"os.name"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         • If Unix‐like:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             – Define `shellExe` = `[0m[32m"/bin/sh"[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor lookup `env.SHELL` as fallback[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             – Define `syntaxFlag` = `[0m[32m"-n"[0m[39m`.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             – Build `ProcessBuilder pb = new [0m[1;35mProcessBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[39mshellExe, syntaxFlag, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"--"[0m[39m, fileName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         • Else [0m[1;39m([0m[39mWindows[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             – Skip external invocation; directly set the metadata [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mmetadata.set[0m[1;39m([0m[39mSHELL_NO_ARGS, false[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and return detection result.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Retain the call `[0m[1;35mpb.directory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtmpDir.toFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Call `[0m[1;35mProcessUtils.execute[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpb, [0m[1;36m20000[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m100000[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m100000[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` exactly as before.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Interpret `exitValue == [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m` as “no‐arg” syntax‐correct script and set [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mmetadata.set[0m[1;39m([0m[39mSHELL_NO_ARGS, true[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, else leave it false.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Update any unit tests or comments referencing the old behavior to note [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“syntax‐only” check.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Ensure `fileName` sanitization [0m[1;39m([0m[39mregex removal of dangerous chars and length [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains in place.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By invoking `[0m[35m/bin/[0m[95msh[0m[39m -n -- fileName`, we preserve the original intent [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mdistinguish scripts that parse successfully without arguments[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m while preventing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mactual code execution of user‐supplied commands.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We use a fixed command vector with no string‐concatenation or shell [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minterpolation, therefore no injection surface remains.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - On Windows, we safely skip dynamic checks, aligning with existing [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcross‐platform Tika behavior [0m[1;39m([0m[39mshebang logic is primarily Unix‐centric[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing ProcessUtils execution, timeouts, and buffers remain untouched, so we[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdo not risk regressions elsewhere.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigations[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Side Effect: Some scripts may parse without executing but still be accepted; [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis is acceptable since we only care about syntax validity and not runtime [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior, matching “no‐arg” semantics.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Side Effect: Windows shell‐detection becomes conservative, possibly [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmisclassifying a “no‐arg” script—but Windows shebangs are rare, and we avoid a [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity risk.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Testing: Add or update tests in ShellCodeDetectorTest covering both Unix and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWindows logic branches, verifying that malformed shebangs or scripts with syntax [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39merrors yield non‐zero exit codes and set `SHELL_NO_ARGS` appropriately.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar safe‐invocation pattern used elsewhere when “bin/sh” is invoked in [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mno‐exec mode [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., CI lint scripts[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - ProcessBuilder API docs caution against concatenating untrusted strings; our [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfixed‐array approach complies with best practices.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mReport[0m===                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The codebase’s ShellCodeDetector class was flagged by Jazzer as vulnerable to OS    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         command injection: it invokes `ProcessBuilder` on untrusted filenames. A patch was  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         attempted that replaces the direct command invocation with a shell “syntax-only”    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         check [1m([0m`[35m/bin/[0m[95msh[0m -n`[1m)[0m on non-Windows platforms, and sets a metadata flag             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         accordingly. After applying the patch, the project fails to compile with a series   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         of “illegal start of type” and “identifier expected” errors in                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `ShellCodeDetector.java`.                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. Initial Issue                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Fuzzer Report: com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical:   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         OS Command Injection                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Stack Trace Highlights:                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • `[1;35mProcessBuilder.start[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` invoked in                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35morg.apache.tika.utils.ProcessUtils.execute[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m`                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Called from `[1;35morg.apache.tika.detect.ShellCodeDetector.detect[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m`           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Ultimately triggered by TikaCLI in a fuzzer harness                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0m`TikaAppUnpackerFuzzer`[1m)[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Impact: Unvalidated filenames or contents could be executed as OS commands,    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         enabling remote code execution.                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. Important Observations                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The vulnerable call lives in `[1;35mShellCodeDetector.detect[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`.                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The code creates a temporary directory, copies the target file, then invokes   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `new [1;35mProcessBuilder[0m[1m([0mfileName[1m)[0m`.                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - There is a `try`[35m/[0m`finally` that deletes the temporary directory, but no        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         intermediate shell sanitization.                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The harness [1m([0mfuzzer[1m)[0m itself is not the root cause—it merely surfaces the       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         vulnerability in production code.                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. Patch Attempt                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Goal: Avoid executing user‐provided scripts directly; instead run a shell      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         syntax check [1m([0m`sh -n`[1m)[0m.                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Key Changes:                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Detect OS via `[1;35mSystem.getProperty[0m[1m([0m[32m"os.name"[0m[1m)[0m`.                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • On Windows, skip syntax check and set `SHELL_NO_ARGS = false`.               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • On Unix‐like systems, build a `[1;35mProcessBuilder[0m[1m([0m[32m"/bin/sh"[0m, [32m"-n"[0m, [32m"--"[0m,         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         fileName[1m)[0m`.                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • If the syntax check returns exit code [1;36m0[0m, set `SHELL_NO_ARGS = true`;         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         otherwise leave it false.                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Retained finally‐block cleanup of the temp directory.                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m. Compilation Log After Patch                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Six errors in `ShellCodeDetector.java` around lines [1;36m120[0m–[1;36m131[0m:                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • “illegal start of type”                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • “identifier expected”                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • “class, interface, enum, or record expected”                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - These indicate misplaced braces or code inserted outside of any method or      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         class scope.                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m. Areas for Further Investigation                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The `[1;35mShellCodeDetector.detect[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` method wrapper: verify opening and closing    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         braces around the `try`, `if/else`, and `finally` blocks.                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The surrounding context in `ShellCodeDetector.java` to ensure the new code is  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         inside the correct method.                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - References to `[1;35mProcessUtils.execute[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` and its exception handling.          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - How `SHELL_NO_ARGS` metadata is used downstream.                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The OS‐detection logic for Windows vs. Unix to confirm that code paths remain  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         inside valid Java blocks.                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview of the root cause  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The compilation errors [0m[1;39m([0m[39m“illegal start of type”, “identifier expected”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m stem [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom misplaced braces in the last patch. By inserting the OS‐detection and [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshell-syntax logic between lines [0m[1;36m97[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m109[0m[39m without adjusting the existing [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`try`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`finally` and return statements, the patch closed the `[0m[1;35mdetect[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprematurely. Subsequent code ended up outside any method or class, causing the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msyntax errors.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Key objectives for the fix  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Keep all new logic inside the `[0m[1;35mdetect[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method’s scope, before the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`return SHELL_SCRIPT;`.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Preserve the single `finally` block that always deletes the temporary [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Avoid executing the user-provided script directly; instead, run `[0m[35m/bin/[0m[95msh[0m[39m -n [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-- <fileName>` on Unix‐like systems.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m On Windows, conservatively leave the no-args metadata flag false.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Set the `SHELL_NO_ARGS` metadata exactly once, after the syntax check but [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore returning.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   f[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Do not alter the public API, the return type [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`MediaType`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, or any [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness/test code.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Step-by-step patch strategy  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m At the top of `ShellCodeDetector.java`, add [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif not already present[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      `import java.util.Locale;`  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m In the `[0m[1;35mdetect[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream, Metadata[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method, locate the block starting at [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe copy into the temp directory [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m97[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Remove only the old lines that [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeal with `[0m[1;35mProcessBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfileName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, its `try/finally`, and the immediate metadata[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msetting, up to the existing `return SHELL_SCRIPT;`.  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Immediately after `[0m[1;35mFiles.copy[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtis.getPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, tmpFile, [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mStandardCopyOption.REPLACE_EXISTING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`, insert the following code snippet, ensuring[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproper indentation and brace pairing:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Determine shell-syntax status safely[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      String osName = [0m[1;35mSystem.getProperty[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"os.name"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toLowerCase[0m[1;39m([0m[39mLocale.ROOT[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      boolean shellNoArgs = false;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mosName.contains[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"win"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              ProcessBuilder pb = new [0m[1;35mProcessBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"/bin/sh"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"-n"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"--"[0m[39m, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfileName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mpb.directory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtmpDir.toFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              FileProcessResult result = [0m[1;35mProcessUtils.execute[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpb, [0m[1;36m20000[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m100000[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m100000[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mresult.getExitValue[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  shellNoArgs = true;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Ignore syntax-check failures; shellNoArgs remains false[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m finally [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mFileUtils.deleteDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtmpDir.toFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mmetadata.set[0m[1;39m([0m[39mSHELL_NO_ARGS, shellNoArgs[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Preserve the original return value[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      return SHELL_SCRIPT;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Remove any extra closing brace [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that was accidentally inserted by the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevious patch before the old `finally` or after line [0m[1;36m119[0m[39m. There should be exactly [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mone closing brace to end the `[0m[1;35mdetect[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method, followed by the `[0m[1;35misShell[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhelper, and finally one closing brace for the class.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Verify that after the inserted snippet, the next lines are:[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m private MediaType [0m[1;35misShell[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains unchanged[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      private MediaType [0m[1;35misShell[0m[1;39m([0m[39mboolean isShell[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[33m...[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification of the approach  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All new code remains inside the existing `[0m[1;35mdetect[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method, so class and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod scopes remain valid.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A single `try`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`finally` block covers shell invocation and directory cleanup, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmatching the original pattern.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We only import `java.util.Locale`, a standard JDK class, to normalize OS [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnames.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We rely on `[0m[1;35mProcessUtils.execute[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, as in other detectors [0m[1;39m([0m[39msee [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FileCommandDetector`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, avoiding direct OS calls.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The patch does not touch harness code, test code, or external libraries, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserving existing functionality and tests.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By setting `shellNoArgs` based on exit code, we replicate the desired metadata[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior without exposing command-injection vectors.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential side effects and mitigation  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If an exception is thrown before the `finally`, the directory is still cleaned[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mup, as intended.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Windows paths always yield `[0m[33mshellNoArgs[0m[39m=[0m[35mfalse[0m[39m`, which downstream logic must [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandle [0m[1;39m([0m[39munchanged from the patch intention[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Performance impact: one extra small process invocation on Unix; this was the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moriginal goal of the patch.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Compilation sanity checks  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure only one `return SHELL_SCRIPT;` exists in the method.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Verify import of `java.util.Locale` at the top.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run `mvn compile` followed by `mvn test` to confirm no regressions.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm the fuzzer no longer reports OS command injection, but the codebase [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompiles cleanly.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
